        <div class="article">
         <a id="a6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39ab087200b">
         </a>
         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html">
           <strong>
            Grossberg:
            <em>
             Using The Step Transaction Doctrine To Attack Tax Shelters
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;Grossberg: &lt;em&gt; Using The Step Transaction Doctrine To Attack Tax Shelters&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;Grossberg: &lt;em&gt; Using The Step Transaction Doctrine To Attack Tax Shelters&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           Jonathan Grossberg (American),
           <a href="https://papers.ssrn.com/sol3/papers.cfm?abstract_id=3198843" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Attacking Tax Shelters: Galloping Toward a Better Step Transaction Doctrine
           </a>
           , 78  La. L. Rev.  369 (2018):
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Since the beginning of the Internal Revenue Code, taxpayers have sought to lower their tax bills through creative tax planning. The step transaction doctrine is one of several tools used by the Internal Revenue Service and courts to challenge tax shelters and tax evasion. The step transaction doctrine provides that the courts may combine two or more allegedly separate steps in a multi-step transaction into a single step to better reflect the economic reality of the taxpayer’s actions. Derived from Supreme Court decisions in the 1930s, the doctrine deserves renewed scrutiny today because serious conceptual issues exist regarding the three current tests that courts use to determine when to combine various steps in a tax-motivated multiple-step transaction. This Article addresses two perennial themes in tax law: the role of judicial doctrines in a statutory system and the difficulty of taxing related-party transactions.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 21, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/scholarship/">
            Scholarship
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/tax/">
            Tax
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html">
            Permalink
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/grossberg-using-the-step-transaction-doctrine-to-attack-tax-shelters.html#comments">
            Comments (0)
           </a>
          </p>
         </div>

        <div class="article">
         <a id="a6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37adec9200d">
         </a>
         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/judge-grants-prosecutors-motion-for-joint-trial-of-markel-murder-suspects-but-warns-be-careful-what-.html">
           <strong>
            Judge Grants Prosecutors' Motion For Joint Trial Of Markel Murder Suspects, But Warns 'Be Careful What You Wish For'; Post July 18, 2014 Statements Are Now Inadmissible As Evidence
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>

         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39abe66200b-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="Markel" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39abe66200b img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39abe66200b-350wi" style="width: 349px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="Markel"/>
           </a>
           Tallahassee Democrat,
           <a href="https://eu.tallahassee.com/story/news/2018/06/20/joining-markel-suspects-could-prove-problematic-evidence/714247002/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Dan Markel Murder: Merging of Suspects' Trials Could Prove Problematic For Evidence
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Prosecutors may not be able to use key statements they say help connect two people to the murder-for-hire plot to kill Florida State law professor Dan Markel.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Sigfredo Garcia and Katherine Magbanua will be tried together after prosecutors succeeded in getting their murder, conspiracy to commit murder and solicitation to commit murder cases joined Wednesday.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           But now statements made after the murder was committed and the $100,000 that Tallahassee investigators say they were paid to commit the crime may not be allowed to be presented at their Oct. 8 trial.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           “I’d put it in the category of be careful what you wish for,” Leon Circuit Judge James Hankinson warned Assistant State Attorney Georgia Cappleman prior to his ruling. “I’m not sure the state really wants to be in the posture where they cannot introduce statements after payment is made.”
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Hankinson said that the conspiracy ended when money changed hands. Statements between two people that implicate others in a conspiracy cannot be introduced as evidence at trial.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/judge-grants-prosecutors-motion-for-joint-trial-of-markel-murder-suspects-but-warns-be-careful-what-.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>

         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37aca24200d-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="Florida Coastal (2017)" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37aca24200d img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37aca24200d-300wi" style="width: 300px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="Florida Coastal (2017)"/>
           </a>
           Following up on
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/florida-coastal-school-of-law-seeks-restraining-order-against-aba.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            yesterday's post
           </a>
           :  Law.com,
           <a href="https://www.law.com/dailybusinessreview/2018/06/20/judge-denies-florida-coastal-law-schools-tro-bid-against-aba/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Judge Denies Florida Coastal Law School's TRO Bid Against ABA
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           A federal judge has declined to issue a temporary restraining order—at least for now—that would have stopped the American Bar Association from requiring Florida Coastal School of Law to make several public disclosures about its accreditation status and bar pass rates.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Judge Brian Davis of the U.S. District Court for the Middle District of Florida ruled June 18 that the ABA should be given an opportunity to respond to the arguments from the Jacksonville school and its owner, InfiLaw Corp., that the disclosures are misleading and would undermine the school’s efforts to recruit more qualified students and boost its bar pass rates.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/federal-judge-denies-florida-coastal-law-schools-tro-bid-against-the-aba.html#more">

         <a id="a6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad3549d33200c">
         </a>
         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html">
           <strong>
            <em>
             Containing Systemic Risk By Taxing Banks Properly
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Containing Systemic Risk By Taxing Banks Properly&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Containing Systemic Risk By Taxing Banks Properly&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           Mark Roe (Harvard) &amp; Michael Troege (ESCP Europe),
           <a href="http://yalejreg.com/nc/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly-by-mark-roe-and-michael-troege/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Containing Systemic Risk By Taxing Banks Properly
           </a>
           , 35 Yale J. on Reg. 181 (2018):
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Tax specialists normally don’t focus on financial stability and financial regulators and analysts typically do not focus on taxes. This is too bad because the corporate tax structure affects financial stability and does so significantly, as we analyze in this article.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           The reason is simple: tax rules influence the capital structure choices of corporations in general and banks in particular, by allowing tax benefits to debt—principally the deductibility of interest—that equity lacks. Today, the corporate tax penalizes equity finance and subsidizes debt relative to equity. As a consequence, corporations overall use more debt than they would in a tax-neutral world.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 20, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/scholarship/">
            Scholarship
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/tax/">
            Tax
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/containing-systemic-risk-by-taxing-banks-properly.html">
            Permalink
           </a>

           </a>
          </p>

        <div class="article">
         <a id="a6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad354be00200c">
         </a>
         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html">
           <strong>
            <em>
             A Simple Low-Cost Institutional Learning-Outcomes Assessment Process For Law Schools
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;A Simple Low-Cost Institutional Learning-Outcomes Assessment Process For Law Schools&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;A Simple Low-Cost Institutional Learning-Outcomes Assessment Process For Law Schools&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           Andrea Anne Curcio (Georgia State),
           <a href="https://papers.ssrn.com/sol3/papers.cfm?abstract_id=3192040" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            A Simple Low-Cost Institutional Learning-Outcomes Assessment Process
           </a>
           , 67 J. Legal Educ. 489 (2018):
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Law school institutional learning outcomes require measuring nuanced skills that develop over time. Rather than look at achievement just in our own courses, institutional outcome-measures assessment requires collective faculty engagement and critical thinking about our students’ overall acquisition of the skills, knowledge, and qualities that ensure they graduate with the competencies necessary to begin life as professionals. Even for those who believe outcomes assessment is a positive move in legal education, in an era of limited budgets and already over-burdened faculty, the new mandated outcomes assessment process raises cost and workload concerns. This essay addresses those concerns. It describes a relatively simple, low-cost model to measure institutional law school learning outcomes that does not require any initial changes in individual faculty members’ pedagogical approach or assessment methods.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 20, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/legal-education/">
            Legal Education
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html">
            Permalink
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-simple-low-cost-institutional-learning-outcomes-assessment-process-for-law-schools-1.html#comments">

           </a>
          </p>

         <a id="a6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37a926d200d">
         </a>
         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html">
           <strong>
            <em>
             We Should Tax The Clintons And Other Former Senior Government Employees At A Higher Rate
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;We Should Tax The Clintons And Other Former Senior Government Employees At A Higher Rate&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;We Should Tax The Clintons And Other Former Senior Government Employees At A Higher Rate&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           Limor Riza (Ono Academic College),
           <a href="https://papers.ssrn.com/sol3/papers.cfm?abstract_id=3107769" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Should We Tax the 'Clintons' and Other Former Senior Civil Servants More? Yes, We Should
           </a>
           , 18  U.C. Davis Bus. L.J. 109 (2017):
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           This paper debates whether former civil servants should be taxed differentially. It argues that whenever public officials’ post-retirement income in the private sector is derived from their previous office, an additional tax should be levied on them, since in such situations the ability-to-pay principle is an insufficient horizontal equity criterion. This idea is grounded in equity propositions and may be justified by various liberal theories of equal opportunities and utilitarianism.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 20, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/scholarship/">
            Scholarship
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/tax/">
            Tax
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html">
            Permalink
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/we-should-tax-the-clintons-and-other-former-senior-government-employees-at-a-higher-rate.html#comments">
            Comments (2)
           </a>
          </p>

         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html">
           <strong>
            <em>
             Why Are Women Underrepresented In Publications In Top Journals?
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Why Are Women Underrepresented In Publications In Top Journals?&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Why Are Women Underrepresented In Publications In Top Journals?&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p>
           Inside Higher Ed,
           <a href="https://www.insidehighered.com/news/2018/06/12/study-editors-major-political-science-journals-demonstrate-no-systematic-bias" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Gender Gap Without Gender Bias
           </a>
           ?:
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           A major political science
           <a href="https://www.cambridge.org/core/journals/ps-political-science-and-politics/article/gender-in-the-journals-publication-patterns-in-political-science/07452099DCDCBF378D233FF402C97DEA" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            study
           </a>
           from last year explored publication patterns across 10 prominent journals, finding a significant gap in publication rates for men and women. The gap couldn’t be explained away by a low overall share of women in the field, the article said, prompting soul-searching among editors about whether they were biased against female authors.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           A new
           <a href="https://www.cambridge.org/core/journals/ps-political-science-and-politics/information/gender-in-the-journals-continued-evidence-from-five-political-science-journals" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            <em>
             PS: Political Science &amp; Politics
            </em>
            report
           </a>
           involving self-audits at five major journals suggests that editorial practices are not, in fact, biased against women. While positive, the findings are also disconcerting, since it remains unclear as to why women are underrepresented as authors in esteemed journals in the discipline.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 20, 2018   |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html">
            Permalink
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/wht-are-women-underrepresented-in-publications-in-top-journals.html#comments">
            Comments (1)
           </a>
          </p>

         </a>
         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html">
           <strong>
            Miller:
            <em>
             Advice For Jeff Bezos — Social Welfare Organizations As Grantmakers
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;Miller: &lt;em&gt; Advice For Jeff Bezos — Social Welfare Organizations As Grantmakers&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;Miller: &lt;em&gt; Advice For Jeff Bezos — Social Welfare Organizations As Grantmakers&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           David S. Miller (Proskauer Rose, New York),
           <a href="https://papers.ssrn.com/sol3/papers.cfm?abstract_id=3198759" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Advice for Jeff Bezos: Social Welfare Organizations as Grantmakers
           </a>
           , 21 N.Y.U. J. Legis. &amp; Pub. Pol'y ___ (2018):
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           This paper responds to Jeff Bezos’ request for philanthropic ideas, but with a suggestion for the structure of his grant making. Gifts of appreciated stock should be made to section 501(c)(3) organizations only to the extent that Bezos will be able to use the charitable deduction that the donation generates before it expires. A social welfare organization should receive all other gifts of appreciated stock.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 20, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/scholarship/">
            Scholarship
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/tax/">
            Tax
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html">
            Permalink
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/miller-advice-for-jeff-bezos-social-welfare-organizations-as-grantmakers.html#comments">

           </a>
          </p>

         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/allard-the-future-of-the-legal-profession.html">
           <strong>
            Allard:
            <em>
             The Future Of The Legal Profession
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/allard-the-future-of-the-legal-profession.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/allard-the-future-of-the-legal-profession.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;Allard: &lt;em&gt; The Future Of The Legal Profession&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/allard-the-future-of-the-legal-profession.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/allard-the-future-of-the-legal-profession.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;Allard: &lt;em&gt; The Future Of The Legal Profession&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/allard-the-future-of-the-legal-profession.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           Nick Allard (
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/05/brooklyn-law-school-parts-ways-with-dean.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Departing Dean
           </a>
           , Brooklyn), Remarks At the St. Petersburg International Legal Forum (SPILF VII) on
           <em>
            The Future of the Legal Profession
           </em>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Prime Minister Medvedev, Justice Minister Konovalov, distinguished guests of the St. Petersburg international legal forum, it is an honor to be invited to participate again, for the sixth time, in the St. Petersburg international legal forum which is a unique global, forward- looking collaborative initiative promoting better understanding of the future of law. If I were forced to use only one word to describe the future changes of the legal profession, I would choose the word “inevitable.” The legal profession and legal educators—always slow and even resistant to adaptation—must evolve with the times. Standing still, clinging to the “business as usual” status quo is not an option.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/allard-the-future-of-the-legal-profession.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 20, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/legal-education/">

             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;Rossman: &lt;em&gt; In Search Of Smarter Homeowner Subsidies&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/rossman-in-search-of-smarter-homeowner-subsidies.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           Matthew J. Rossman (Case Western),
           <a href="https://papers.ssrn.com/sol3/papers.cfm?abstract_id=3069048">
            In Search of Smarter Homeowner Subsidies
           </a>
           , 40 U. Haw. L. Rev. 270 (2017):
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Critics have long assailed the federal tax code’s principal homeowner subsidies as lucrative tax breaks for upper income households that are essentially worthless to those financially constrained from purchasing a home. This article examines the subsidies through a different lens and reveals another serious flaw. It demonstrates how the homeowner subsidies, which represent a massive federal investment in homeownership, do very little to contain and instead probably increase costs on others that result from certain types of housing choices and that other federal policies seek to remedy. These negative housing externalities include: (i) blight, deterioration, and public health risks in disinvested housing markets, (ii) an array of individual and societal harms associated with heightened economic and racial housing segregation, (iii) environmental degradation, and (iv) taxpayer funded disaster relief for those who reside in environmental hotspots. In effect, the subsidies pay for housing choices that the government later pays to cleans up after.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           This article provides several explanations for this disconnect. Among these is an idealization of homeownership, reflected in the tax code, which sees only its benefits. Accordingly, the subsidies reward homeowner decisions at large and are insensitive to the varying amounts of positive and negative externalities that follow from particular types of homeowner choices. For this reason, the article contends that the current subsidies are not “smart.”
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/rossman-in-search-of-smarter-homeowner-subsidies.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 20, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/scholarship/">
            Scholarship
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/tax/">
            Tax
           </a>
           |

           </a>
          </p>
         </div>

         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p>
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad3547989200c-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="SMY" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad3547989200c img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad3547989200c-300wi" style="width: 300px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="SMY"/>
           </a>
           Law.com,
           <a href="https://www.law.com/2018/06/19/in-a-first-yale-and-stanford-law-journals-team-up-for-metoo-project/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            In a First, Yale and Stanford Law Journals Team Up for #MeToo Project
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           The #MeToo movement has highlighted the problem of men wielding their workplace power to sexually harass women, but the issue of gender-based harassment and discrimination is much broader and pervasive than the current media narrative allows.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           That’s the takeaway from a new #MeToo Symposium—a collection of 12 essays from leading employment discrimination law experts—published Monday in a collaboration between the
           <a href="https://www.yalelawjournal.org/collection/MeToo" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Yale Law Journal
           </a>
           and the
           <a href="https://www.stanfordlawreview.org/metoo-symposium/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Stanford Law Review
           </a>
           .
          </p>
          <p>

         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/charitable-giving-and-the-tax-cuts-and-jobs-act.html">
           <strong>
            <em>
             Charitable Giving And The Tax Cuts And Jobs Act
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">

            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>

               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/charitable-giving-and-the-tax-cuts-and-jobs-act.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Charitable Giving And The Tax Cuts And Jobs Act&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/charitable-giving-and-the-tax-cuts-and-jobs-act.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/charitable-giving-and-the-tax-cuts-and-jobs-act.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Charitable Giving And The Tax Cuts And Jobs Act&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/charitable-giving-and-the-tax-cuts-and-jobs-act.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39a1e68200b-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="AEI (2016)" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39a1e68200b img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39a1e68200b-300wi" style="width: 300px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="AEI (2016)"/>
           </a>
           Alex Brill &amp; Derrick Choe (American Enterprise Institute),
           <a href="https://www.aei.org/wp-content/uploads/2018/06/Charitable-Giving-and-the-Tax-Cuts-and-Jobs-Act.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Charitable Giving and the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           This paper investigates how the Tax Cuts and Jobs Act affects household charitable giving in the United States. We find that the law will reduce charitable giving by $17.2 billion (4.0 percent) in 2018 according to a static model and $16.3 billion assuming a modest boost to growth. Four-fifths of this decline is driven by an increase in the number of taxpayers who claim the standard deduction.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/charitable-giving-and-the-tax-cuts-and-jobs-act.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>

         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-college-presidents-twitter-strategy.html">
           <strong>
            <em>
             A College President’s Twitter Strategy
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">

            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-college-presidents-twitter-strategy.html">

               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-college-presidents-twitter-strategy.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;A College President’s Twitter Strategy&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-college-presidents-twitter-strategy.html">

             <li>

               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;A College President’s Twitter Strategy&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-college-presidents-twitter-strategy.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37a3a87200d-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="Ono" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37a3a87200d img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad37a3a87200d-300wi" style="width: 300px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="Ono"/>
           </a>
           Inside Higher Ed,
           <a href="https://www.insidehighered.com/news/2018/06/15/drawing-line-between-policy-and-personality-twitter" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            A College President’s Twitter Strategy
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           The University of British Columbia’s president, Santa Ono, is a social media star among college presidents.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           On Ono’s Twitter feed, there are beautiful pictures of the UBC campus, details of upcoming events and celebrations of the achievements of students and staff.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           When not promoting his institution on Twitter, Ono shares more personal posts: a recommendation for a local ramen bar, a quote from Pablo Picasso or the news that the Harry Potter play just won six Tony Awards.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Mixed in with these promotional and personal posts, however, is the occasional statement of university policy. And that, students say, is a big problem.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/a-college-presidents-twitter-strategy.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>

         <div class="line">

               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;Call For Papers: &lt;em&gt;The Commerce Clause And The Global Economy&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/call-for-papers-the-commerce-clause-and-the-global-economy.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad399ca24200b-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="Chapman Logo (2017)" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad399ca24200b img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad399ca24200b-250wi" style="width: 246px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="Chapman Logo (2017)"/>
           </a>
           The Chapman Law Review is pleased to invite article submissions on the theme:
           <em>
            The Commerce Clause and the Global Economy
           </em>
           . Publications will appear in a symposium edition, and authors will receive an honorarium.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           With the growth of online retailers and the rise of the global marketplace, federal and state governments have been charged with the task of navigating the waters of the global economy and its inevitable collision with the Commerce Clause. In June, the United States Supreme Court is expected to render a decision in
           <em>
            South Dakota v. Wayfair
           </em>
           , in which South Dakota has asked the Court to reconsider its ruling in
           <em>
            Quill v. North Dakota
           </em>
           and allow states to require out-of-state retailers that do not have a physical presence in the state to collect local sales taxes from their customers. Regardless of the outcome, this case has opened up a series of questions about the scope of the Commerce Clause in an increasingly global economy—specifically the ability of state and local governments to regulate global economic actors in order to protect communities against the adverse effects of globalization.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/call-for-papers-the-commerce-clause-and-the-global-economy.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">

          <p>
           <a href="https://www.cbpp.org/careers/senior-tax-legal-analyst-or-tax-legal-analyst" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
           </a>
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad3541837200c-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="CBPP Logo (2013)" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad3541837200c img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad3541837200c-300wi" style="width: 300px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="CBPP Logo (2013)"/>
           </a>
           <a href="https://www.cbpp.org/careers/senior-tax-legal-analyst-or-tax-legal-analyst" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Senior Tax Legal Analyst or Tax Legal Analyst
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           The Center on Budget and Policy Priorities is a non-profit research organization with a mission to improve the well-being of low- and moderate-income people. The Center has a national reputation for rigorous analysis of fiscal policies and an ability to influence policy debates.   It is widely respected for its expertise on federal budget and tax issues.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           The Center seeks to hire a senior tax legal analyst or tax legal analyst to expand our work to identify examples of tax loopholes, gaming, and unintended consequences under the new tax law and lift these examples up among the tax community, policymakers, media, and the public. Working with other experts on the Federal Fiscal Policy team, the analyst will help to shape and drive public debate on these issues.
          </p>

         <h3>

               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p style="text-align: justify;">
           <a class="asset-img-link" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39a1dd1200b-popup" onclick="window.open( this.href, '_blank', 'width=640,height=480,scrollbars=no,resizable=no,toolbar=no,directories=no,location=no,menubar=no,status=no,left=0,top=0' ); return false" style="float: right;">
            <img alt="Florida Coastal (2017)" class="asset asset-image at-xid-6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39a1dd1200b img-responsive" src="http://taxprof.typepad.com/.a/6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad39a1dd1200b-300wi" style="width: 300px; margin: 0px 0px 5px 5px;" title="Florida Coastal (2017)"/>
           </a>
           Following up on my previous post,
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/05/florida-coastal-law-school-sues-aba-kirkland-ellis-alleges-arbitrary-enforcement-of-accreditation-st.html" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Florida Coastal Law School Sues ABA; Kirkland &amp; Ellis Alleges Arbitrary Enforcement Of Accreditation Standards
           </a>
           :  Law.com,
           <a href="https://www.law.com/2018/06/18/florida-coastal-school-of-law-seeks-restraining-order-against-aba/?kw=Florida%20Coastal%20School%20of%20Law%20Seeks%20Restraining%20Order%20Against%20ABA&amp;et=editorial&amp;bu=Law.com&amp;cn=20180618&amp;src=EMC-Email&amp;pt=AfternoonUpdate" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Florida Coastal School of Law Seeks Restraining Order Against ABA
           </a>
           :
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           Florida Coastal School of Law has asked a federal judge to halt new disclosures the American Bar Association has required the troubled school to make to its students, arguing the requirements will undermine its efforts to improve.
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           In a
           <a href="https://images.law.com/contrib/content/uploads/documents/292/Florida-Coastal-MPI.pdf" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            motion for a temporary restraining order and preliminary injunction
           </a>
           , filed June 15 in U.S. District Court for the Middle District of Florida, Florida Coastal and owner InfiLaw Corp. have asked the court to postpone several requirements the ABA imposed in April after determining that the school is out of compliance with rules pertaining to the rigor or it educational program and its academic support.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/florida-coastal-school-of-law-seeks-restraining-order-against-aba.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>

        <div class="article">
         <a id="a6a00d8341c4eab53ef022ad353f72e200c">
         </a>
         <h3>
          <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html">
           <strong>
            Newman:
            <em>
             Modern Day Lessons From Two New York Tax Opinions By Benjamin Cardozo
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>
            Share
           </a>
           <div class="dropdown clearfix">
            <div class="tab-arrow">
            </div>
            <ul class="clearfix">
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.facebook.com/sharer.php?u=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html">
               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;Newman: &lt;em&gt; Modern Day Lessons From Two New York Tax Opinions By Benjamin Cardozo&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://plus.google.com/share?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html">
               <i class="icon-google-plus">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://www.linkedin.com/shareArticle?mini=true&amp;url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html">
               <i class="icon-linkedin">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="mailto:?subject=&lt;strong&gt;Newman: &lt;em&gt; Modern Day Lessons From Two New York Tax Opinions By Benjamin Cardozo&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt; on The Taxprof Blog&amp;body=Check this article out on The Taxprof Blog: http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html">
               <i class="icon-envelope">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
           </div>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="hidden-phone">
          <p>
           Joel S. Newman (Wake Forest),
           <a href="https://papers.ssrn.com/sol3/papers.cfm?abstract_id=3194736" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            Two New York Tax Cases
           </a>
           , 34 Touro L. Rev. 301 (2018):
          </p>
          <p style="margin: 15px 0px; padding: 0px; border: 0px none; outline: 0px none; font-size: 14px; vertical-align: baseline; background-color: #ebf0f3; line-height: 20px; color: #363636; font-family: Arial,Helvetica,sans-serif; font-style: normal; font-variant: normal; font-weight: normal; letter-spacing: normal; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0px; text-transform: none; white-space: normal; word-spacing: 0px;">
           While he was on the New York Court of Appeals, Benjamin Cardozo wrote a number of opinions on state tax issues.
           <a href="https://casetext.com/case/people-ex-rel-studebaker-corporation-v-gilchrist" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
            People ex rel. Studebaker Corp. v. Gilchrist
           </a>
           was an early transfer pricing case. Studebaker Corporation established a number of sales subsidiaries, so that income could be shifted away from states with corporate franchise taxes. As a result of its manipulation, a net loss of over $400,000 was reported to New York State in 1920, even though Studebaker earned a profit of over $11 million nationwide. The New York State Tax Commission and the Appellate Division reallocated the income, but the Court of Appeals reversed. Cardozo disagreed with the method of allocation used below. However, his opinion left the door open for reallocations in subsequent cases. Curiously, the facts would have lent themselves to transfer pricing analysis, which is used in modern international tax cases, rather than the formulary apportionment used by the courts below, which has become the standard method in state cases.
          </p>
          <p>
           <a class="btn btn-small" href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html#more">
            Continue reading
            <i class="icon-double-angle-right">
            </i>
           </a>
          </p>
          <p class="posted">
           June 19, 2018 in
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/scholarship/">
            Scholarship
           </a>
           ,
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/tax/">
            Tax
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html">
            Permalink
           </a>
           |
           <a href="http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/newman-lessons-from-two-new-york-tax-opinions-by-benjamin-cardozo.html#comments">
            Comments (0)
           </a>
          </p>
         </div>

            <em>
             Google Now Displays Acceptance, Cost And Graduation Data In College Search Results
            </em>
           </strong>
          </a>
         </h3>
         <div class="line">
          <p class="author">
           By
           <a href="#">
            Paul Caron
           </a>
          </p>
          <div class="share hidden-phone">
           <a href="#">
            <i class="icon-share">
            </i>

           </a>

               <i class="icon-facebook">
               </i>
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="http://twitter.com/intent/tweet?url=http://taxprof.typepad.com/taxprof_blog/2018/06/google-now-displays-acceptance-cost-and-graduation-data-in-college-searche-results.html&amp;text=&lt;strong&gt;&lt;em&gt;Google Now Displays Acceptance, Cost And Graduation Data In College Search Results&lt;/em&gt;&lt;/strong&gt;&amp;via=SoCalTaxProf">
               <i class="icon-twitter">
